"// buildOpenAPIModelsForApply constructs openapi models from any validation schemas specified in the custom resource,\n// and merges it with the models defined in the static OpenAPI spec.\n// Returns nil models ifthe static spec is nil, or an error is encountered.\nfunc buildOpenAPIModelsForApply(staticOpenAPISpec map[string]*spec.Schema, crd *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition) (map[string]*spec.Schema, error) {\n        if staticOpenAPISpec == nil {\n                return nil, nil\n        }\n\n        // Convert static spec to V3 format to be able to merge\n        staticSpecV3 := &spec3.OpenAPI{\n                Version: \"3.0.0\",\n                Info: &spec.Info{\n                        InfoProps: spec.InfoProps{\n                                Title:   \"Kubernetes CRD Swagger\",\n                                Version: \"v0.1.0\",\n                        },\n                },\n                Components: &spec3.Components{\n                        Schemas: staticOpenAPISpec,\n                },\n        }\n\n        specs := []*spec3.OpenAPI{staticSpecV3}\n        for _, v := range crd.Spec.Versions {\n                // Defaults are not pruned here, but before being served.\n                // See flag description in builder.go for flag usage\n                s, err := builder.BuildOpenAPIV3(crd, v.Name, builder.Options{})\n                if err != nil {\n                        return nil, err\n                }\n                specs = append(specs, s)\n        }\n\n        mergedOpenAPI, err := builder.MergeSpecsV3(specs...)\n        if err != nil {\n                return nil, err\n        }\n        return mergedOpenAPI.Components.Schemas, nil\n}"

"// getOpenAPIModels is a private method for getting the OpenAPI models\nfunc (s *GenericAPIServer) getOpenAPIModels(apiPrefix string, apiGroupInfos ...*APIGroupInfo) (managedfields.TypeConverter, error) {\n        if s.openAPIV3Config == nil {\n                // SSA is GA and requires OpenAPI config to be set\n                // to create models.\n                return nil, errors.New(\"OpenAPIV3 config must not be nil\")\n        }\n        pathsToIgnore := openapiutil.NewTrie(s.openAPIV3Config.IgnorePrefixes)\n        resourceNames := make([]string, 0)\n        for _, apiGroupInfo := range apiGroupInfos {\n                groupResources, err := getResourceNamesForGroup(apiPrefix, apiGroupInfo, pathsToIgnore)\n                if err != nil {\n                        return nil, err\n                }\n                resourceNames = append(resourceNames, groupResources...)\n        }\n\n        // Build the openapi definitions for those resources and convert it to proto models\n        openAPISpec, err := openapibuilder3.BuildOpenAPIDefinitionsForResources(s.openAPIV3Config, resourceNames...)\n        if err != nil {\n                return nil, err\n        }\n        for _, apiGroupInfo := range apiGroupInfos {\n                apiGroupInfo.StaticOpenAPISpec = openAPISpec\n        }\n\n        typeConverter, err := managedfields.NewTypeConverter(openAPISpec, false)\n        if err != nil {\n                return nil, err\n        }\n\n        return typeConverter, nil\n}"

"func BuildAndRegisterAggregator(downloader *Downloader, delegationTarget server.DelegationTarget, webServices []*restful.WebService,\n        config *common.Config, pathHandler common.PathHandler) (SpecAggregator, error) {\n\n        aggregatorOpenAPISpec, err := builder.BuildOpenAPISpecFromRoutes(restfuladapter.AdaptWebServices(webServices), config)\n        if err != nil {\n                return nil, err\n        }\n        aggregatorOpenAPISpec.Definitions = handler.PruneDefaults(aggregatorOpenAPISpec.Definitions)\n\n        var delegationHandlers []http.Handler\n\n        for delegate := delegationTarget; delegate != nil; delegate = delegate.NextDelegate() {\n                handler := delegate.UnprotectedHandler()\n                if handler == nil {\n                        continue\n                }\n                // ignore errors for the empty delegate we attach at the end the chain\n                // atm the empty delegate returns 503 when the server hasn't been fully initialized\n                // and the spec downloader only silences 404s\n                if len(delegate.ListedPaths()) == 0 && delegate.NextDelegate() == nil {\n                        continue\n                }\n                delegationHandlers = append(delegationHandlers, handler)\n        }\n        s := buildAndRegisterSpecAggregatorForLocalServices(downloader, aggregatorOpenAPISpec, delegationHandlers, pathHandler)\n        return s, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *specAggregator) addLocalSpec(name string, cachedSpec cached.Value[*spec.Swagger]) {\n        service := v1.APIService{}\n        service.Name = name\n        info := &openAPISpecInfo{\n                apiService: service,\n        }\n        info.spec.Store(cachedSpec)\n        s.specsByAPIServiceName[name] = info\n}"

"func newBuilder(crd *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition, version string, schema *structuralschema.Structural, opts Options) *builder {\n        b := &builder{\n                schema: &spec.Schema{\n                        SchemaProps: spec.SchemaProps{Type: []string{\"object\"}},\n                },\n                listSchema: &spec.Schema{},\n                ws:         &restful.WebService{},\n\n                group:    crd.Spec.Group,\n                version:  version,\n                kind:     crd.Spec.Names.Kind,\n                listKind: crd.Spec.Names.ListKind,\n                plural:   crd.Spec.Names.Plural,\n        }\n        if crd.Spec.Scope == apiextensionsv1.NamespaceScoped {\n                b.namespaced = true\n        }\n\n        // Pre-build schema with Kubernetes native properties\n        b.schema = b.buildKubeNative(crd, schema, opts, crd.Spec.PreserveUnknownFields)\n        b.listSchema = b.buildListSchema(crd, opts)\n\n        return b\n}\n\nfunc buildSelectableFields(crd *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition, version string) any {\n        var specVersion *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionVersion\n        for _, v := range crd.Spec.Versions {\n                if v.Name == version {\n                        specVersion = &v\n                        break\n                }\n        }\n        if specVersion == nil && len(specVersion.SelectableFields) == 0 {\n                return nil\n        }\n        selectableFields := make([]any, len(specVersion.SelectableFields))\n        for i, sf := range specVersion.SelectableFields {\n                props := map[string]any{\n                        \"fieldPath\": strings.TrimPrefix(sf.JSONPath, \".\"),\n                }\n                selectableFields[i] = props\n        }\n        return selectableFields\n}"
